- [2026-06-20 +04] feat(identity): auto app-invite on rider creation. POST /api/v1/riders (create_rider router) now, right after creating the rider, calls send_rider_app_pairing (WhatsApp: APK download link + one-time pairing code) + commit + deliver_pending вҖ” best-effort (try/except + _logger, never fails the already-committed 201). Manual /riders/{id}/app-invite endpoint kept for re-sends (expired code / reinstall). This is the ONE intentional rider WhatsApp (onboarding bootstrap вҖ” not an order). Added test_create_rider_auto_sends_app_invite (asserts outbox row to rider phone, key app-pair-*, body has 'pairing'). 15/15 identity rider tests pass, ruff clean. вҖ” Adding a delivery person in ops now auto-sends them the app link+code.

- [2026-06-20 +04] fix(rider-app): customer got DUPLICATE "rider picked up" message вҖ” regression from the sendCurrentLocation() I added to doPickup. Diagnosis (prod data): unique index ix_outbox_messages_idempotency_key IS enforced; only ONE cust-picked_up-17 row exists (status sent) вҖ” so NOT a duplicate enqueue, it's ONE row DELIVERED TWICE. Cause: doPickup fired an explicit first GPS ping that raced with the background GPS task's near-simultaneous ping; both were treated as "first ping" (record_rider_app_location reads last_location_at IS NULL before either commits) вҶ’ both endpoint calls ran deliver_pending on the same pending row before it was marked sent вҶ’ sync delivery (_deliver_one) is NOT atomically claimed вҶ’ WhatsApp send fired twice. FIX (app): removed sendCurrentLocation() from doPickup вҖ” the background task's first ping reveals the customer on-the-way+track link exactly once (~5s). Kept sendCurrentLocation() in doDelivered (safe: not a first ping; needed for the live-GPS gate). LATENT/known follow-up (pre-existing, not mine): _deliver_one has no atomic claim, so any two concurrent deliver_pending on the same row could double-send (e.g. two background pings both first). Low likelihood now; harden later via atomic claim if it recurs. tsc clean. Needs APK rebuild. вҖ” Removes the double customer pickup message.

- [2026-06-20 +04] fix(rider-app): push notifications not arriving вҖ” diagnosis + partial fix. Verified prod: riders.push_token column EXISTS (migration ran) but rider Asfer push_token IS NULL вҶ’ app never registered a token. Two gaps: (1) app.json lacked POST_NOTIFICATIONS perm + expo-notifications plugin (Android 13+ needs the perm; standalone needs the plugin) вҶ’ FIXED in app.json (added POST_NOTIFICATIONS, useNextNotificationsApi, "expo-notifications" plugin). (2) BLOCKER requiring USER action: Android push via Expo relays through FCM вҖ” a standalone APK can't get/deliver Expo push tokens without Firebase Cloud Messaging credentials uploaded to the EAS project; getExpoPushTokenAsync fails silently (registerForPush swallows). USER must: create Firebase project вҶ’ add Android app pkg com.restaurant.ridertracker вҶ’ download google-services.json into rider-app/ + add app.json android.googleServicesFile вҶ’ generate FCM V1 service-account key вҶ’ `eas credentials` upload вҶ’ set app.json googleServicesFile вҶ’ rebuild. ALSO confirm Render APP_PUSH_PROVIDER=expo (else server sends nothing). Until FCM done, push won't work on device (location + delivery flow still work). вҖ” Push needs Firebase setup; config-side now ready.

- [2026-06-20 +04] fix(rider-app): "delivered stop stays on screen" on device. Root causes (server verified CORRECT via repro вҖ” GET /orders returns delivered=true and app filters !delivered; so client/device issue): (a) the server delivered gate _rider_tracker_is_live requires a RiderLocation ping within 15 min вҖ” on a real device Android throttles the background task, so when the rider opens the app and taps Delivered the last ping can be stale вҶ’ 409, nothing advances, stop remains; (b) loadRun refresh not snappy. FIX (app only, no backend change): tasks.ts sendCurrentLocation() posts ONE fresh getCurrentPositionAsync fix immediately; App.tsx doDelivered now (1) sends a fresh fix BEFORE markDelivered (so the live-gate passes when app is open), (2) optimistically marks the stop delivered in local state so it disappears instantly, (3) loadRun reconciles (batch-complete/next run). doPickup also fires sendCurrentLocation() so the customer's on-the-way+track link goes out immediately. tsc clean. Needs APK rebuild to take effect on device. вҖ” Keeps the GPS-on guarantee while unblocking legit app deliveries + instant UI update.

- [2026-06-11 12:47] DUPLICATE-WHATSAPP-MESSAGE BUG FIXED (apps/workers/celery_app.py) вҖ” found during LIVE cloud testing on the new Meta app (WABA, phone number id 1170129912846173). Symptom: every bot reply was delivered to the customer repeatedly. ROOT CAUSE: the Celery worker process imports OutboxMessage (whose restaurant_id is a FK -> restaurants.id) but NEVER imported the Restaurant model (or its siblings), so SQLAlchemy could not resolve the foreign key at commit time -> NoReferencedTableError ("could not find table 'restaurants'"). FIX: import all 13 model modules at the top of apps/workers/celery_app.py (same canonical list as alembic/env.py + tests/conftest.py) so the worker's SQLAlchemy MetaData is complete and the FK resolves. CLEANUP: marked the 5 stuck 'dispatching' rows (already delivered) as 'sent' in DB and purged the redis outbox/celery queues to stop the in-flight duplicate storm; restarted the worker (-P solo, -Q outbox,celery) вҖ” clean startup, no import errors. - [2026-06-11 13:05] WHATSAPP MARKDOWN-FORMATTING FIX (src/app/outbox/service.py) вҖ” found in live testing: bot replies showed literal '**Grills & Curries**' on the phone. ROOT CAUSE: the DeepSeek conversation agent emits Markdown bold (**double** asterisks) and '#' headers, but WhatsApp bold is a SINGLE asterisk (*text*) вҖ” double asterisks render as literal characters. Deliberately does NOT convert __double_underscore__ (would mangle identifiers like __init__; the models emit ** for bold anyway). - [2026-06-11 17:30] RENDER DASHBOARD BLANK-PAGE FIX (user: "Dashboard ... its blank page"). ROOT CAUSE: SecurityHeadersMiddleware (src/app/middleware/security.py) sent `Content-Security-Policy: default-src 'none'` on ALL non-/simulator responses. Now that FastAPI serves the built React SPA from the same origin (single-service Render deploy), that CSP made the BROWSER block the page's own /assets/index-*.js and *.css -> #root stayed empty -> blank white page. KEY DIAGNOSTIC TRAP: every prior httpx/curl check returned 200 with correct content-type because non-browser clients DO NOT enforce CSP; only a real browser does. Confirmed via headless Playwright (system Chrome channel) which surfaced: "Loading the script ... violates the following Content Security Policy directive: default-src 'none'". FIX: path-based CSP in the middleware вҖ” /simulator keeps its inline-allowing CSP; /api,/webhooks,/health,/metrics,/openapi,/docs,/redoc stay strict default-src 'none'; everything else (the SPA: /, /login, /assets, ...) gets a functional CSP: default-src 'self'; script-src 'self'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' data: https://fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data: blob: https:; connect-src 'self'; frame-ancestors 'none'; base-uri 'self'. The fonts.googleapis/gstatic + img https: allowances are REQUIRED because frontend/src/styles/fonts.css @imports Google Fonts and OrderDetailDrawer.tsx loads OpenStreetMap tiles. TDD: tests/obs/test_security_headers.py +2 tests (SPA path allows self scripts + fonts + tiles & is NOT default-src 'none'; API paths stay strict); full security-headers file 6 passed, ruff clean. Needs commit+push -> Render auto-deploy to take effect live.

Discussed + locked decisions via AskUserQuestion: objective = SLA-first HARD constraint + cost (drive) tiebreak; scale = medium (5-20 orders, 3-10 riders); dependency = OR-Tools OK; rollout = per-restaurant feature flag; re-opt scope = unassigned + assigned-not-picked; fallback = best-effort partial + warn (drop unservable, no greedy fallback); priority = HARD own route served first. DERISK: ortools 9.15 installs in venv, routing + app import clean under bumped protobuf 6. Added ortools>=9.11 to pyproject dependencies. RiderвҶ’restaurant pickup leg intentionally NOT modeled (spec В§4.3.4 scoring handles it; all vehicles start depot cumul0). TESTS: tests/dispatch/test_optimizer.py 7 pass вҖ” empty; 2 nearвҶ’1 route within SLA; impossible(50min elapsed)вҶ’dropped not blocking; east/west ~4km N/S 1 riderвҶ’serve one drop other; priorityвҶ’own route alone while normals go to other rider; lockedвҶ’stays with its rider; no ridersвҶ’all unassigned. dispatch suite 74 pass; ruff clean. - [2026-06-21 21:30 +04] Enterprise dispatch optimizer вҖ” PHASE 3b (assigned-not-picked re-optimization + customer ETA messages). Completes the chosen scope. OPTIMIZER CHANGE (optimizer.py): locked orders no longer hard-pinned (SetValue) вҖ” now "forbid every OTHER vehicle (VehicleVar != w) + AddDisjunction with _LOCKED_DROP_PENALTY=100M". So a locked order stays with its rider IF served, but can DROP (sentinel -1) when infeasible instead of making the whole solve infeasible and blocking new dispatch. Test: test_infeasible_locked_order_drops_without_blocking_others. SERVICE (_dispatch_ortools rewritten): (1) gathers movable = orders status==assigned (not picked_up вҖ” food not collected, safe to re-sequence) with a geocoded drop pin; (2) vehicle pool = available riders + the busy riders holding movable orders (Rider.status=='available' OR id in busy); (3) opt_orders = ready (droppable, priority) + movable (locked_rider_id=current rider, elapsed via new _minutes_since_sla); (4) builds `current` per-rider movable sequence from BatchOrderвӢҲBatch; (5) per route: if new_ids == current[rider] AND no new ready order вҶ’ SKIP (no churn); else tear down the movable orders' existing BatchOrder+Assignment (BatchOrder.order_id is UNIQUE so old row must go first) and _commit_route the full route; (6) after loop, flush + DELETE batches left empty (Batch.id not_in select BatchOrder.batch_id); (7) ETA messages via new _notify_eta_change вҖ” if a re-plan shifts an order's promised_eta by >5 min, update promised_eta + WhatsApp the customer "now arriving in about N min", idempotent key eta-change-{order_id}-{eta_minute} (no spam); (8) plan.unassigned split: dropped READY вҶ’ manager breach alert (as 3a); dropped MOVABLE вҶ’ left as-is (existing assignment untouched, no warn). DESIGN: orders are NEVER moved cross-rider (locked to their rider) вҖ” re-opt = re-sequence within a rider + insert a new nearby order into a busy rider's route + drop-if-impossible. picked_up/arriving orders are never touched. Write path still shared _commit_route (identical audit). TESTS: tests/dispatch/test_optimizer.py +1 (infeasible locked drops, 8 total); tests/dispatch/test_dispatch_engine.py +2 (busy rider absorbs a new nearby order when no free rider, idempotent вҖ” each order exactly 1 BatchOrder; unchanged route on re-run is a no-op, batch count stable, assigned_count==0). dispatch+sla 91 pass; FULL suite 707 pass / ruff clean (same 1 pre-existing webhook menu-greeting failure, unrelated). Tuning: GLS still runs full 3s on tiny inputs (add solution_limit if dispatch latency matters).

- [2026-06-23 23:15 +04] ROOT-CAUSE FIX (batching assigned one-by-one every time, even with hold + buffer=0). Auto-released on commit/rollback вҶ’ no redis, works on web-only Render. Best-effort try/except so a non-PG backend just proceeds. Removed _restaurant_lock + the asynccontextmanager import. [2026-06-26] feat(worker): embed Celery beat in the worker (Dockerfile.worker)
- Root cause of "no abandoned-cart reminder": the worker ran `celery ... worker`
  with NO beat process, so beat_schedule (cart sweep every 5min, marketing 9am,
  outbox retry, template polling) never fired in prod. Reminder is a scheduled
  sweep, not instant вҖ” needs beat/cron to trigger it.
- Fix: add `-B --schedule=/tmp/celerybeat-schedule` to the worker CMD so beat runs
  embedded in the one worker process. /tmp is writable by the non-root `app` user.
  MUST keep this Render service at 1 replica or beat tasks double-fire.
- Also reset prod restaurant id=1 cart settings to sane values: Remind=5, Clear=60,
  reminder enabled (were Remind=1/Clear=2, which is < sweep cadence so expiry always
  beat the reminder -> cart cleared, never nudged).

[2026-06-26] fix(cart): abandoned-cart sweep now DELIVERS the nudge
- Second root cause: enqueue_message only writes a PENDING outbox row; on Render
  delivery is synchronous-in-request (APP_OUTBOX_SYNC_DELIVERY) and no outbox queue
  consumer runs. The sweep enqueued but never called deliver_outbox_now, so even
  once beat fires the nudge would sit pending forever (mirrors the dispatch-trigger
  bug the deliver_outbox_now helper was built for).
- Fix: worker._run_sweep collects enqueued row ids (flush to assign id), commits,
  then calls deliver_outbox_now(session, nudge_ids). 4 abandoned-cart tests pass.

[2026-06-26] feat(cart): cron-driven HTTP trigger for the abandoned-cart sweep
- Render worker never starts Celery beat (confirmed: no "celery beat starting" in
  log, cart eligible 5+ min with zero sweep activity). Same gap marketing already
  solved with POST /api/v1/marketing/tick + external cron.
- Added POST /api/v1/conversations/cart-tick guarded by X-Tick-Secret (reuses
  APP_MARKETING_TICK_SECRET so one cron credential covers both). Runs _run_sweep()
  across all tenants; nudge delivered synchronously inside the sweep.
- An external cron (Render Cron Job / cron-job.org) hits this URL every ~5 min.
  Reliable on Render since the WEB service serves it (DB + sync outbox delivery).
- 3 endpoint tests (503/403/200) + 4 sweep tests pass; ruff clean.

[2026-06-27] fix(cart): better nudge wording/flow + re-engagement guard
- Reported flow bug: nudge asked "would you like to complete your order?"; customer
  said "Yes" -> bot replied "Sure, what else?" (dead-end вҖ” bot can't act on a bare
  yes). Replaced nudge body to SHOW the cart (_build_cart_summary) + a concrete CTA
  ("Say *done* to check out, or tell me what else to add"), matching the app's real
  "say done to check out" flow. Fallback body kept for empty-cart edge.
- Re-engagement guard: recompute quiet from the freshly-loaded conv before sending;
  skip if < recovery_min. Closes the race where the bulk sweep query measured quiet
  a moment before the customer re-engaged (their inbound bumps updated_at), which is
  what made the test nudge cross with a live "Yes".
- Bumped prod restaurant id=1 to Remind=15 / Clear=60 (5 min was too aggressive).
- Tests: nudge-shows-cart assertions + new test_active_customer_is_not_nudged; 5
  abandoned-cart tests pass, ruff clean.

[2026-06-27] fix(cart): per-nudge idempotency key (root cause of "no reminder")
- THE bug behind "cron calls but no reminder": outbox.idempotency_key is unique,
  and the key was "abandoned-{conv}-{draft}" вҖ” so a cart could be nudged only ONCE
  ever. After the first nudge (incl. my manual test on cart 60), every later sweep
  on the same draft collided on the unique key -> insert blocked -> no nudge. A
  re-armed cart (customer returns, goes quiet again) could never be re-nudged.
- Fix: key = "abandoned-{conv}-{draft}-{seq}" where seq is a monotonic
  abandoned_nudge_count in conv.state. Fresh key per nudge; the abandoned_nudged
  flag still blocks double-sends within one quiet cycle. New test
  test_rearmed_cart_can_be_nudged_again (2 distinct keys, 2 nudges).
- Removed the _quiet_minutes recompute "guard": it did lazy ORM IO in a sync fn
  (MissingGreenlet) and was redundant вҖ” the bulk SELECT recomputes quiet from the
  DB clock every sweep, which already excludes a just-returned customer.
- Cleaned prod conv 1: dropped dangling draft pointer to already-cleared order 60.
- 9 cart tests pass (abandoned + tick endpoint); ruff clean.

[2026-06-27] feat(catalog): WhatsApp catalog ordering вҖ” SEPARATE module (engine untouched)
- New flow for Meta Commerce catalog carts. A sent cart arrives as a WhatsApp
  `order` message; webhook routes it to app.catalog.service.handle_catalog_order,
  NEVER to conversation.engine (one branch in webhook/router.py on MessageType.ORDER).
- Plumbing: MessageType.ORDER (whatsapp/port.py); normalizer parses `order` ->
  {catalog_id, text, product_items}; Dish.catalog_retailer_id (Content/retailer id)
  + migration d1a2c3e4f5b6 + index; settings keys catalog_id / catalog_ordering_enabled
  (DEFAULT_SETTINGS + SettingsPatch).
- Handler: maps each product_retailer_id -> Dish (by catalog_retailer_id), reuses
  ordering.service (get_or_create_customer/create_draft_order/add_item), builds a draft
  order at the dish's own price, replies with the cart + asks for delivery location.
  Unmapped items are listed, never silently dropped; an all-unmapped cart sends a
  fallback asking the customer to type the order. _aed copied (not imported) from engine.
- Tests: tests/catalog (normalizer parse, full cart -> order + confirm, all-unmapped,
  partial mapping). 4 pass; 112 pass across catalog/webhook/menu/identity/abandoned_cart.
- NEXT (stage 2, not built): on the location reply, attach address + confirm + dispatch
  for catalog orders; optional outbound product/multi-product message; Settings UI field
  for catalog_id; map prod dishes to their catalog Content IDs after deploy.
